# Roadmap

Version-by-version history of `adam`, grouped into two architectural eras. The final entry (v1.0.0) is the MVP cut.

## Lifecycle view

```
  v0.1.0 ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ v0.4.0           v0.4.5 ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ v1.0.0
  ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ transformer era ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§            ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ FST + dialog era ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§
  ‚Ēā                              ‚Ēā            ‚Ēā                            ‚Ēā
  corpus curation                ‚Ēā            deterministic FST morphology ‚Ēā
  BPE tokenizer                  ‚Ēā            14 k-entry pure Kazakh Lexicon
  24.2 M transformer             ‚Ēā            25-intent dialog pipeline    ‚Ēā
  (archived as reference)        ‚Ēā            trilingual input, KZ output  ‚Ēā
                                 v            FST-guaranteed morphology    v
                              pivot                                       MVP
```

The transformer era (v0.1‚Äďv0.4) established the corpus, tokenizer, and training infrastructure. The FST + dialog era (v0.4.5+) replaced the stochastic model with a deterministic pipeline that holds predictability as a hard constraint. The v0.4.0 checkpoint is preserved in `data/training/` as a regression reference but is not on the v1.0.0 codepath.

## Phase 10 ‚ÄĒ FST + dialog layer (v0.4.5 ‚Üí v1.0.0)

The MVP path. Each release is strictly additive ‚ÄĒ no rollbacks, no feature gating.

| Release | Scope | Result |
|---|---|---|
| v0.4.5 | `adam-kernel-fst` crate ‚ÄĒ phonology + morphotactics + parser + lexicon + CLI | 55 unit tests, 100% roundtrip on 36,238 full-lexicon cycles |
| v0.5.0 | Participles, converbs, vowel-final-stem aorist coalescence | 68 unit tests; most non-finite Kazakh verb forms covered |
| v0.5.5 | Pure Kazakh lexicon ‚ÄĒ drop 1,500 loanwords, add 500 Abai-attested classical roots | 14,106 entries, Abai coverage 88.8% ‚Üí 97.8% |
| v0.6.0 | Derivational morphology ‚ÄĒ 11 word-formation suffixes | 78 unit tests; root‚Üíderived‚Üíinflected chains work end-to-end |
| v0.7.0 | First dialog layer ‚ÄĒ `adam-dialog` crate, 5-intent MVP, `adam_chat` CLI | 175 workspace tests; 5-layer predictable pipeline |
| v0.7.5 | Dialog widening to 10 intents; templates moved to `data/dialog/templates/v1.toml` | 183 workspace tests; data-driven template repo |
| v0.8.0 | 25 intents (+15: age, location, occupation, family, weather, time, compliment, request, well-wishes, statement-of-name); PersonName extraction | 201 workspace tests; first entity extraction lands |
| v0.8.5 | Multi-turn session state via `Conversation`; greeting `{name}` variants | 204 workspace tests; "Say your name once, get greeted forever" |
| v0.9.0 | Full entity absorption ‚ÄĒ Kazakh numeral parser (1‚Äď99), ablative/locative city, 1sg-copula occupation; `{age}/{city}/{occupation}` slots | 215 workspace tests; every statement contributes a remembered entity |
| v0.9.5 | FST-backed slot expansion ‚ÄĒ `{slot\|features}` parsed and rendered via `synthesise_noun`; cross-slot templates | 229 workspace tests; agreement becomes FST-guaranteed |
| v0.9.6 | Multilingual recogniser ‚ÄĒ Kazakh / Russian / English triggers for all 25 intents; Latin-root safety guard | 245 workspace tests |
| v0.9.7 | Lexicon-backed occupation recognition via generic 1sg-copula stripping + POS lookup | 251 workspace tests |
| v0.9.8 | Full slot syntax (Derivation + Possessive) + Latin‚ÜíCyrillic transliteration + triple-slot templates | 265 workspace tests; demo-ready UX |
| v0.9.9 | FST Instrumental harmony fix (`–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č–ľ–į–Ĺ ‚Üí –ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ`, `–ľ“Ī“ď–į–Ľ—Ė–ľ–Ī–Ķ–Ĺ ‚Üí –ľ“Ī“ď–į–Ľ—Ė–ľ–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ`); 6 regression tests; template polish | 271 workspace tests; last stretch before MVP |
| v1.0.0 | **MVP cut** ‚ÄĒ no new features; full documentation refresh; transformer-era narrative compressed into history section | 271 workspace tests; investor-demoable |
| v1.1.0 | **Kazakh-only revert + modern Lexicon + smart Unknown** ‚ÄĒ reverted v0.9.6 multilingual triggers, removed transliteration module; added Insult intent; Unknown handler extracts noun hint via FST; +12 modern Kazakh Lexicon roots | 253 workspace tests; course-correction toward thinking Kazakh model |
| v1.1.5 | **Corpus audit baseline** ‚ÄĒ new `corpus_audit` binary measures the v1.x starting position per-source: word counts, vocab, Kazakh purity, dedup. Reports **2.24 M words baseline** (45√ó expansion needed to reach the 100 M target). Adds expansion plan through v1.5.0 | 256 workspace tests; measurable progress toward thinking model |
| v1.2.0 | **Classical literature expansion** ‚ÄĒ new `kazakh_classics_pack.json` (111 samples, 926 words, **100.00 % Kazakh purity**) from –ę–Ī—č—Ä–į–Ļ –ź–Ľ—ā—č–Ĺ—Ā–į—Ä–ł–Ĺ + –ú–į“ď–∂–į–Ĺ –Ė“Ī–ľ–į–Ī–į–Ķ–≤ (kk.wikisource, public domain). OCR deferred | 256 workspace tests; literary core added |
| v1.3.0 | **Wikipedia re-extract** ‚ÄĒ rewrote `process_wikipedia_kz` (byte-by-byte ‚Üí 64 KB chunked streaming, 100√ó faster; added 10 % loanword-density filter). Committed pack: 150 k samples / 1.61 M words / 99.99 % purity. Local uncapped: 1.4 M samples / 15 M words. Corpus total 2.85 M words, expansion gap 45√ó ‚Üí 35√ó | 256 workspace tests; +27 % corpus |
| v1.3.5 | **Sharding + docs drift + v2.0 direction committed** ‚ÄĒ `--full` mode writes 10 shards (‚Č§50 MB each) to gitignored `data/curated/shards/` for local retrieval-engine fuel; `corpus_audit --local` scans them. Docs fixed: badge 253‚Üí256, `foundation_scope` no longer claims trilingual/transliteration, "FST-guaranteed" wording tightened. **v2.0 committed as retrieval-over-corpus, not a trained LM** | 256 workspace tests; local corpus 16 M words, gap to 100 M = 6.2√ó |
| v1.4.0 | **FST-NER + DST + predicate-copula FST** ‚ÄĒ added `Predicate` feature to `NounFeatures` (7 person variants + 6 suffix templates); +30 Kazakh place-name entries in Lexicon; `detect_statement_of_location` / `detect_statement_of_occupation` refactored to use `Analysis` as primary path; `Conversation` gained `active_intent` + `intent_history` + `resolve_follow_up` | 262 workspace tests; closes Codex/Antigravity critiques |
| v1.4.5 | **Lexicon polish +20 nouns** ‚ÄĒ modern Kazakh professions (–Ĺ“Ī—Ā“õ–į—É—ą—č, –ļ–Ķ“£–Ķ—Ā—ą—Ė, –∂–Ķ—ā–Ķ–ļ—ą—Ė, –∂“Į—Ä–≥—Ė–∑—É—ą—Ė, —Ā–į—É–ī–į–≥–Ķ—Ä, ‚Ä¶) and common conversational vocabulary (”ô–ļ–Ķ, –į“ď–į, –į–Ņ–į, –Ī“Į–≥—Ė–Ĺ, –Ķ—Ä—ā–Ķ“£, –ļ–Ķ—ą–Ķ, –ľ–Ķ–ļ–Ķ–ľ–Ķ, –ļ–Ķ“£—Ā–Ķ, “Ī–Ļ—č–ľ). All native Kazakh, no loanwords | 262 workspace tests; each new profession round-trips through FST-NER |
| v1.5.0 | **CC-100 re-extract** ‚ÄĒ rewrote `process_cc100_kk` (stdin streaming, old 50 k cap removed, 10 % loanword-density filter, sharding at 140 k samples/shard). Committed pack: 140 k samples / 4.01 M words committed. 33 local shards (02‚Äď34) add 4.6 M samples / 74 M more local words. **Corpus: 4.01 M committed / 77.9 M local; gap to 100 M = 1.3√ó**. Purity ‚ąí1.6 pp (web-crawl tax, accepted per corpus-purity directive) | 262 workspace tests; +27√ó local corpus |
| v1.5.5 | **Morpheme-coverage audit** ‚ÄĒ new `morpheme_coverage` binary. Prefix-matches every committed word against the 14,247-root Lexicon, reports per-pack coverage + top 20 uncovered words by frequency. Baseline: **79.48 % across 3.84 M committed words** (synthetic 99.82 %, real-corpus packs 76‚Äď81 %). Concrete Lexicon gaps identified: `–ī–Ķ–Ņ`, `–ĺ—Ā—č`, `–ĺ–Ĺ—č“£`, `–ī–Ķ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ`, `–Ņ–Ķ–Ĺ`, `–ĺ—Ä—ā–į`. v1.5.5 was originally planned as "government sources"; that directive moves to v1.6.x since the sources need dedicated scraping infrastructure | 267 workspace tests; coverage delta now a measurable PR metric |
| v1.6.0 | **Retrieval engine bootstrap** ‚ÄĒ new `adam-retrieval` crate with `MorphemeIndex` (BTreeMap for deterministic JSON) + `SampleRef` + `search` + `search_conjunction`. New `build_morpheme_index` binary parses committed packs through the FST (unique-word cache ‚Üí ~10 min full-corpus build). Two modes: default `--limit 500/pack` writes the committed 1.6 MB snapshot; `--full` writes the gitignored 700 MB full index. FST throughput measured at 1.155 ms/word. No `Intent::Unknown` integration yet (v1.6.5+) | 274 workspace tests; retrieval crate shipped |
| v1.6.5 | **Retrieval wired into Intent::Unknown** ‚ÄĒ `MorphemeIndex` gains `sample_texts` so dialog can cite the actual sentence, not just the sample id. `Conversation::with_morpheme_index` attaches the index; when Unknown fires with a recognised noun, the response quotes a verbatim corpus example. New `unknown.with_evidence` template family wraps quotes in ¬ę‚Ä¶¬Ľ. Deterministic: picks the first (sorted) posting ‚ÄĒ reproducible across runs. No regression: without an index, v1.1.0 noun-echo behaviour is preserved | 279 workspace tests; dialog now cites Abai, Wikipedia, CC-100 for its fallback turns |
| v1.7.0 | **Deterministic retrieval ranking** ‚ÄĒ `MorphemeIndex::rank` replaces "first posting" with a composite score: **0.40¬∑overlap + 0.30¬∑pack_purity + 0.15¬∑length_goodness ‚ąí 0.15¬∑loanword_density**. Dialog ranks over every content root (`content_roots`), not just the first. Editorial pack priors hardcode classical > curated > Wikipedia > web. Visible effect: ¬ę–ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā–Ķ–Ņ –ļ–Ķ—Ä–Ķ–ļ –Ņ–Ķ¬Ľ now cites an 8-word sentence instead of a 36-word bureaucratic paragraph. Zero randomness, zero training; ties break by `(pack, sample_id)` | 286 workspace tests; retrieval engine starts behaving like a search engine |
| v1.8.0 | **Session-aware compositional synthesis (option A: frame-only)** ‚ÄĒ retrieved quote stays verbatim (zero fabrication risk); frame around it becomes session-aware. When user has `name`/`city`/`age`/`occupation` remembered, planner prefers a template that personalises the citation (¬ę–°—Ė–∑, –Ē”ô—É–Ľ–Ķ—ā, –Ī–į–Ľ–į —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č —Ā“Ī—Ä–į–Ņ —ā“Ī—Ä—Ā—č–∑ –Ī–į‚Ä¶¬Ľ instead of just ¬ę–Ī–į–Ľ–į —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č‚Ä¶¬Ľ). Implemented as pure templates ‚ÄĒ no planner logic change, no new crate. `template_is_fillable` auto-activates session-aware variants when slots exist. Known bug: `-–ľ—č–Ĺ` greedy-strip in occupation recogniser (v1.8.5 fix) | 288 workspace tests; composition implemented as pure data |
| v1.8.5 | **Locative+P1Sg bug fix + FST-aware city slots + README refresh** ‚ÄĒ fixed `detect_statement_of_occupation` to reject Locative/Ablative cases (so ¬ę–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ –ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č–ī–į–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ ‚Üí `city: –ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č`, not `occupation: –į–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č`); `detect_statement_of_location` now accepts bare Locative+P1Sg without requiring a separate verb. Wired `{city|locative}` into 2 retrieval templates so ¬ę–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č–ī–į —ā“Ī—Ä–į—ā—č–Ĺ —Ā—Ė–∑–≥–Ķ‚Ä¶¬Ľ renders with harmony-correct locative suffix (no more dangling `–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č-–ī–į`). Comprehensive README refresh bringing all version refs, badges, capabilities, specs, history and out-of-scope lists in sync with the v1.5.0‚Äďv1.8.0 retrieval-era arc | 290 workspace tests; +2 regression tests |
| v1.9.0 | **In-sample city swap (option B, opt-in, year-guarded)** ‚ÄĒ new `adam-retrieval::compose` module with `compose_with_city(sample, user_city, lexicon)` ‚Üí `Composition` carrying provenance per `Swap`. Closed editorial list `PLACE_NAMES` (20 Kazakh cities); user's city must also be in the list. Biographical-year guard refuses the whole swap on any 4-digit year in [1500, 2100] to keep biographies untouched. New `ComposeMode { Verbatim, InSampleCitySwap }` on `Conversation` with `with_compose_mode(...)` ‚ÄĒ default stays `Verbatim` (v1.8.5 behaviour, byte-identical corpus quote). `InSampleCitySwap` rewrites city mentions inside the cited quote to the user's city via FST feature-preserving synthesis. Grammaticality FST-guaranteed, semantic truthfulness no longer guaranteed ‚ÄĒ option B trade-off is explicit and auditable | 301 workspace tests; +8 compose unit + +3 dialog e2e |
| v1.9.5 | **Composition-marker framing (adapted-evidence family)** ‚ÄĒ restores the traceability contract broken in v1.9.0. `Intent::Unknown` gains `example_adapted: bool`; when `true` the planner routes to the new `unknown.with_adapted_evidence` family whose every template contains the ¬ę–Ī–Ķ–Ļ—Ė–ľ–ī-¬Ľ stem (¬ę–Ī–Ķ–Ļ—Ė–ľ–ī–Ķ–Ľ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ –Ĺ“Ī—Ā“õ–į¬Ľ, ¬ę“õ–į–Ľ–į“£—č–∑“ď–į –Ī–Ķ–Ļ—Ė–ľ–ī–Ķ–Ņ –ļ”©—Ä–ī—Ė–ľ¬Ľ). `maybe_compose` now returns `(String, bool)` so the swap flag propagates cleanly. Two trust-critical tests enforce: (a) swap ‚Üí marker fires, (b) no swap ‚Üí marker NEVER fires ‚ÄĒ no false claims of adaptation. The user can always distinguish a verbatim corpus quote from an adapted one by grepping for ¬ę–Ī–Ķ–Ļ—Ė–ľ–ī-¬Ľ | 303 workspace tests; +2 e2e guarantees |
| v2.0.0 | **v2.0 commitment release ‚ÄĒ investor-demoable** ‚ÄĒ not a feature drop, an architectural commitment: `project_retrieval_not_neural_v2` is now frozen. New `adam_demo` scripted 15-turn walkthrough (3 parts ‚ÄĒ verbatim, opt-in swap with guards, synthetic swap showing the marker). `adam_chat` now auto-loads the morpheme index and exposes `--compose` / `--no-retrieval` flags. New `docs/architecture_v2.md` as single canonical reference. README gains a "Why adam" comparison table vs mainstream LLMs. Explicit commitments declared: not a trained model, not multilingual, not generative, not a generalist, not self-modifying | 303 tests pass (unchanged); 0 new tests ‚ÄĒ v2.0 adds binaries + docs on top of the v1.9.5 library surface |
| v2.1.0 | **ILMRR bootstrap ‚ÄĒ fact extraction** ‚ÄĒ first step toward reasoning. New `adam-reasoning` crate with typed `Fact { subject, predicate, object, pattern, source, confidence, raw_text }`. `Predicate` enum starts with `IsA` + `LivesIn`. `ConfidenceKind` is categorical evidence (Grammar, CuratedQuote, RepeatedPattern, HumanApproved, RuleInferred) ‚ÄĒ **not an LLM probability**. Two pattern matchers: copula `X ‚ÄĒ Y` with strict single-token LHS + head-extracted RHS (right-to-left FST scan resolves "Y-—Ā—Ė" ‚Üí root Y); locative-existential `X Y-–ī–į —ā“Ī—Ä–į–ī—č` with `Case::Locative` + `—ā“Ī—Ä—É`-verb + bare-nominative subject. New `extract_facts` binary (default / `--full` / `--limit N` modes, streamed progress). Baseline on committed corpus: **11 facts from 3,191 samples, 7 precise + 4 Lexicon-gap signals** (–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ—č“õ, –∂–į–Ĺ–į—ą—č, –Ī–į—Ā—ā–į—É, –Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į—ą–į“õ) ‚Üí concrete v2.2 agenda. All facts provenance-carrying back to `(pack, sample_id)`. Zero regressions elsewhere | 325 workspace tests (+22 reasoning); first structured knowledge artifact `data/retrieval/facts.json` |
| v2.2.0 | **Lexicon pollution purge + `Has` predicate** ‚ÄĒ the v2.1 feedback loop paid off. Scan found **87 intervocalic-voicing-duplicate root pairs** in segmentation_roots.json (–ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ņ‚ÜĒ–ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ī, —Ā–į–Ī–į“õ‚ÜĒ—Ā–į–Ī–į“ď, –Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į—ą–į“õ‚ÜĒ–Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į—ą–į“ď ‚Ä¶), all Apertium-import artefacts. Purged 87 + added 3 missing roots (–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ—č“õ, –Ī–į—Ā—ā–į—É, –∂–į–Ĺ–į—ą—č—Ä). Zero code references to any of the 87 IDs ‚Üí no regressions. New third pattern matcher `possessive_has`: `X-—ā—č“£ Y-—Ā—č –Ī–į—Ä` ‚Üí `Has` via `Case::Genitive` + `Possessive::P3` + existential `–Ī–į—Ä` + adjacency guard. New `Predicate::Has` variant. Extraction: 11‚Üí13 facts, 1‚Üí2 distinct predicates; 3 of 4 v2.1 imprecisions corrected (—č–Ĺ—ā—č–ľ–į“õ‚Üí–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ—č“õ, –Ī–į–Ľ–į‚Üí–Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į—ą–į“õ, –į–Ĺ–į‚Üí–∂–į–Ĺ–į—ą—č—Ä); 1 remains (–∂–Ķ—Ä‚Üí–Ī–į—Ā—ā–į—É blocked by vowel-final+P3 FST bug, filed for v2.3). Lexicon delta: 4516‚Üí4432 roots (‚ąí84, cleaner) | 328 workspace tests (+3 possessive); 13 facts, 2 predicates |
| v2.3.0 | **FST glide-vowel fix + Lexical Graph v0** ‚ÄĒ Kazakh `—É`, `–ł`, `—é` moved from `ConsonantClass::VowelPreceding` to `HighSonorant` (aligning code with enum docstring). Fixes vowel-final + P3 mis-synthesis: `–ĺ“õ—É+P3` = –ĺ“õ—É—č (not –ĺ“õ—É—Ā—č), `–Ī–į—Ā—ā–į—É+P3` = –Ī–į—Ā—ā–į—É—č. v2.2's last imprecision (–∂–Ķ—Ä ‚Üí –Ī–į—Ā—ā–į—É) now resolves correctly. New `adam_reasoning::graph::LexicalGraph` ‚ÄĒ pure projection of `facts.json` into `(nodes, edges)` with provenance on every edge. `build_lexical_graph` binary emits `data/retrieval/lexical_graph.json`. Extraction delta: 13‚Üí**15 facts, 0 imprecisions**. Graph state: 29 nodes, 15 edges, most-connected `–Ī“Ī–Ľ–į“õ` (degree 2). Zero regressions; 335 tests (+7 graph) | 335 workspace tests; 15 facts with 0 imprecisions + first lexical graph artifact |
| v2.4.0 | **Rule reasoner v0 (forward-chaining) + docs-currency audit** ‚ÄĒ new `adam_reasoning::reasoner` + `run_reasoner` binary. 1 active rule (`R1_is_a_transitivity`: A IsA B ‚ąß B IsA C ‚üĻ A IsA C), 4 documented for v2.5+. Every derived fact carries `rule_id`, non-empty `source_chain`, and `ConfidenceKind::RuleInferred` (never `Grammar`). Test-enforced trust invariants: derived ‚áí rule-inferred confidence; fixpoint reached ‚áí idempotent; tautology (A IsA A) never emitted. Honest baseline: **0 derivations on current 15 facts** ‚ÄĒ reasoner correctly wired (unit tests verify 3-hop chains), data doesn't yet form chains; v2.5 patterns will populate middle nodes. Plus: comprehensive docs-currency audit (13 files refreshed ‚ÄĒ Cargo descriptions, crate lib.rs docstrings, foundation_scope, corpus_audit, repository_layout, eval_baseline, architecture_v2, dialog README, lexicon README, dialog architecture history), new `feedback_docs_currency` memory codifies the per-release checklist | 343 workspace tests (+8 reasoner); first rule-inference artifact `data/retrieval/derived_facts.json` |
| v2.5.0 | **`GoesTo` predicate + dative-motion pattern (v3.0 ladder step 1/6)** ‚ÄĒ first rung of the committed v2.5 ‚Üí v3.0 ladder toward investor-demoable intelligent MVP. New `Predicate::GoesTo`, new `patterns::dative_goes_to` (X Y-–ļ–Ķ –Ī–į—Ä–į–ī—č ‚Üí GoesTo; type-checked on `Case::Dative` + verb root `–Ī–į—Ä—É` + bare-nominative subject; closed-class and tautology guards). `LexicalGraph::from_facts` now handles `goes_to` string; `unreachable!` arm enforces compile-time branch-completeness for future predicate variants. 0 firings on the committed 3191 samples (proverbs + metaphors rarely use dative-motion), pattern verified by 4 unit tests. Zero regressions | 347 workspace tests (+4 dative tests); 15 facts unchanged; graph and derived artefacts regenerated |
| v2.6.0 | **`PartOf` + `RelatedTo` predicates + R5 rule active (v3.0 ladder step 2/6)** ‚ÄĒ the reasoner starts producing real derivations. Two new predicate variants. R5 rule (`A IsA X ‚ąß B IsA X ‚üĻ RelatedTo(A, B)`, symmetric with canonical-pair dedup) activates. First real derivation on the v2.5 fact set: `–ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ņ RelatedTo —Ė–Ľ—Ė–ľ` (both IsA –Ī“Ī–Ľ–į“õ across two different proverbs ‚Üí related). Graph projection handles both new predicate strings with the existing compile-time `unreachable!` safety arm. Zero regressions | 352 workspace tests (+5 R5 + predicate stability); derived_facts.json now contains 1 real inference |
| v2.7.0 | **Dialog integration: reasoning chains in `Intent::Unknown` (v3.0 ladder step 3/6)** ‚ÄĒ the reasoner's output becomes user-visible. `Conversation` gains `derived_facts` + `extracted_facts` fields + `with_reasoning_chains(...)` builder. `Intent::Unknown` gains `reasoning_chain: Option<String>`. Pure renderer `render_derivation_as_kazakh` produces Kazakh prose with the mandatory ¬ę–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā-¬Ľ trust marker. Planner routes to new `unknown.with_derived_chain` family (4 templates, all with ¬ę–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā-¬Ľ) when a chain fires. `adam_chat` autoloads `facts.json` + `derived_facts.json` at startup. End-to-end demo: `adam_chat --once "–ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ņ —ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č –Ī—Ė—Ä–ī–Ķ“£–Ķ –į–Ļ—ā"` ‚Üí ¬ę–ļ—Ė—ā–į–Ņ –Ņ–Ķ–Ĺ —Ė–Ľ—Ė–ľ –Ī—Ė—Ä-–Ī—Ė—Ä—Ė–Ĺ–Ķ –Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ¬Ľ. Test-enforced trust invariants: chain match ‚áí marker fires; no derived_facts ‚áí marker NEVER fires across 32 seeds (mirrors v1.9.5's verbatim-never-claims-adapted). Zero regressions | 354 workspace tests (+2 e2e); first user-visible inference in adam's history |
| v2.8.0 | **R2 Has-inheritance + complete predicate renderers (v3.0 ladder step 4/6)** ‚ÄĒ activates `R2_has_inheritance` (A IsA B ‚ąß B Has X ‚üĻ A Has X, tautology-guarded, `ConfidenceKind::RuleInferred` labelled for consumer-side monotonic-inheritance scepticism). Fills out `render_derivation_as_kazakh` ‚ÄĒ every `Predicate` variant (IsA, LivesIn, Has, GoesTo, PartOf, RelatedTo) now produces a specific Kazakh phrasing with the mandatory ¬ę–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā-¬Ľ marker; exhaustive match, no generic fallback. On current 15-fact corpus: R2 fires 0 (no outgoing Has edges from IsA targets ‚ÄĒ awaits pattern density from future releases). | v5.15.0 | **V1 ‚ÄĒ VAD continuous listening + compound-utterance split.** Minor-version release. Second voice-arc milestone. Two complementary capabilities. **Energy-based VAD:** new fields on `MicConfig` (`vad_enabled` default true / `vad_silence_after_speech` 1500 ms / `vad_amplitude_threshold` 0.02√ói16::MAX / `vad_min_speech_before_silence` 600 ms); `MicConfig::push_to_talk()` preset opts out. New public method `MicCapture::wait_for_vad_stop` blocks main thread until silence-after-speech > threshold OR max_duration fires; returns `VadStopReason` enum. Algorithm: poll shared buffer every 30 ms, compute RMS over 30-ms frames, classify speech vs silence by amplitude threshold. Silence detection arms only after 600 ms cumulative speech (prevents premature stop on first intra-syllable pause). Zero new dependencies. **Multi-clause utterance splitter:** new `discourse::split_compound_utterance` splits input on Kazakh sentence-boundary punctuation (`,` / `.` / `;` / `!` / `?` / `‚Ä¶`) ‚ÄĒ quote-aware (¬ę‚Ä¶¬Ľ), code-block-aware (` ``` `). | v5.6.0 | **Performance ‚ÄĒ parallel load + streaming JSON parse.** Minor-version release closing the cold-start performance arc. Two architectural changes work together. **Layer 1 ‚ÄĒ parallel load:** `adam_chat::main` spawns 5 `std::thread`s (retrieval index, reasoning chains, suffix priors, root affinity, world_core) instead of loading sequentially. Total cold-start time approaches `max(individual)` not `sum`. Conversation builder still waits for all threads ‚ÄĒ no lazy-load delay on first user query. **Layer 2 ‚ÄĒ streaming JSON parse:** switched from `read_to_string` + `from_str` (which holds the entire file as `String` alongside the parsed struct at peak) to `BufReader::new(File::open)` + `from_reader`. Applied to `adam_chat::load_retrieval_index`, `adam_chat::load_reasoning_chains`, `RootAffinity::load`, `SuffixPriors::load`. Cuts peak by ~70 MB across the 5 artefacts. **Measurable impact:** cold start (warm cache) **0.38 s ‚Üí 0.22-0.28 s (27‚Äď45 % faster ‚úÖ <500 ms target)**; max RSS **230 MB ‚Üí 160 MB (31 % reduction ‚úÖ <200 MB target)**; peak memory **225 MB ‚Üí 154 MB (32 % reduction)**; p50 turn latency **21.42 ms ‚Üí 21.57 ms (unchanged ‚úÖ no regression)**. **Why x.y.0:** new runtime architecture for cold-start + new peak-memory profile affecting every binary + two library API surface changes (`RootAffinity::load`, `SuffixPriors::load` now use `BufReader`) together justify minor-version. **Deferred:** lazy load on first use (would save additional ~50 MB but adds first-query latency; not needed since both targets already met); binary serialization format. **Verified:** workspace 1 205 passing (unchanged); fmt + check clean. Stripe ‚ÄĒ Deterministic AI research (cold-start performance arc; both targets met without behavioural regression). | 1205 (unchanged) |

| v5.2.0 | **Kazakh grapheme-to-phoneme (G2P) module ‚ÄĒ substrate for kernel-pure concatenative TTS.** First step toward fully-deterministic Kazakh pronunciation that doesn't depend on neural models or external TTS. New module [`adam_dialog::phoneme`](../crates/adam-dialog/src/phoneme.rs) maps Kazakh Cyrillic text to a stream of `Phoneme` units via rule-based G2P. **Phoneme inventory:** 10 vowels (–į ”ô –Ķ –ł —č —Ė –ĺ ”© “Ī “Į) + 23 consonants (–Ī –Ņ –ľ —É —Ą —ā –ī –Ĺ —Ā –∑ –Ľ —Ä –ļ “õ –≥ “ď —Ö “Ľ —ą –∂ —á –Ļ “£) ‚ÄĒ 33 phonemes total. Russian-loan compounds decomposed: —Ď‚Üíj+o, —é‚Üíj+u, —Ź‚Üíj+a, —Ü‚Üít+s, —Č‚Üí É+t É. Hard/soft signs (—ä —Ć) silent. **API:** `Phoneme` enum + `text_to_phonemes(text) -> Vec<Phoneme>` + `phonemes_to_ipa(stream) -> String` + `Phoneme::is_vowel()` / `bank_id()` (ASCII-safe filename for future phoneme bank). v5.2.0 ships only the G2P module ‚ÄĒ useful for educational tools (phonemic transcription), phoneme-aware spell-checking, and future PhonemeBankTtsBackend. The actual phoneme bank (audio WAV per phoneme) is a separate content investment deferred to v5.2.5+. **Regression tests:** 20 new ‚ÄĒ vowel classification, IPA-symbol uniqueness, bank_id ASCII-safety, simple words (¬ę–į–Ľ–ľ–į¬Ľ / ¬ę“õ“Ī—Ā¬Ľ / ¬ę–ļ”©–Ļ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ¬Ľ / ¬ę—ā–į“£¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į¬Ľ / ¬ę–Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—ą—č–Ľ—č“õ¬Ľ), Russian-loan decomposition, hard/soft sign drop, whitespace/punctuation drop, uppercase normalisation, mixed Cyrillic+Latin. **Verified:** workspace **1121 passing** (+20 from new v5.2.0 phoneme tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 5.2.0 green; fmt + build clean. world_core: 3003 / 3245 / 30892 unchanged. **Strategic:** TTS arc (v5.0.0 + v5.0.5 + v5.1.0 + v5.2.0) builds toward kernel-pure Kazakh voice ‚ÄĒ research direction nobody else pursues because OS-bundled or neural TTS are ¬ęgood enough¬Ľ for everyone except a project that explicitly wants offline-deterministic auditable pronunciation. **Roadmap (next):** v5.2.5 phoneme bank recording (native-speaker audio + `PhonemeBankTtsBackend`); v5.3.0+ open. Stripe ‚ÄĒ Kazakh school tutor (kernel-pure pronunciation substrate). | 1121 (+ 20 v5.2.0 phoneme tests) |
| v5.1.0 | **Optional Piper neural TTS backend ‚ÄĒ richer voice for users who want it.** Second `TtsBackend` implementation alongside v5.0.0 OS-native default. Users who want noticeably more natural speech can install [Piper](https://github.com/rhasspy/piper) (~5 MB CLI binary) and download a voice model (~50-100 MB ONNX), then run `adam_chat --tts --tts-backend piper --tts-model <path>`. Architecturally fenced: Piper bundled NEITHER in adam binary NOR in repo ‚ÄĒ purely opt-in, kernel determinism unchanged. **What's added:** new [`PiperTtsBackend`](../crates/adam-dialog/src/tts.rs); `detect(model_path)` returns None if piper / audio player / ONNX model missing; pipeline `text ‚Üí piper stdin ‚Üí temp WAV ‚Üí spawn audio player`; audio player tracked in Mutex for kill-previous (mirrors v5.0.5); helper `locate_command(name)` resolves PATH via `which`; `locate_audio_player()` probes `afplay ‚Üí aplay ‚Üí paplay ‚Üí play`. REPL flags `--tts-backend piper` + `--tts-model <path>` with graceful fallback to OS backend on detection failure. **Smoke test:** `adam_chat --once ... --tts --tts-backend piper --tts-model /nonexistent.onnx` correctly logs fallback message and speaks via OS Aru voice. **Regression tests:** 7 new ‚ÄĒ piper backend describe/accessors/detect-with-missing-model/empty-input-no-op + locate_command on real binary / missing binary / locate_audio_player on macOS. **Verified:** workspace **1101 passing** (+7 from new v5.1.0 tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 5.1.0 green; fmt + build clean. world_core: 3003 / 3245 / 30892 unchanged. **Strategic:** for current macOS users, bundled `Aru` voice is already excellent ‚ÄĒ Piper is for Linux users without quality TTS or experimentation. | v5.0.5 | **Non-blocking TTS dispatch ‚ÄĒ REPL stays responsive while adam speaks.** Builds on v5.0.0 voice output. Pre-v5.0.5 `OsTtsBackend::speak` blocked the REPL until the synthesiser finished ‚ÄĒ student could only type next input *after* adam stopped speaking. Post-v5.0.5 the synthesiser runs as a detached child process; `speak()` returns in microseconds, REPL accepts the next prompt immediately. **Latest-wins semantics:** if the student types a new query while a previous response is still being spoken, the previous synthesis is killed and the new one starts. **Touches:** [`tts.rs`](../crates/adam-dialog/src/tts.rs) ‚ÄĒ `OsTtsBackend` gains private `Mutex<Option<Child>>`; `speak()` switches `Command::status()` ‚Üí `Command::spawn()`; kill+wait reaps previous child first. New `new()` constructor + `program()` / `args()` / `voice()` accessors. `Drop` impl best-effort reaps last child on REPL exit. **Regression tests:** 3 new ‚ÄĒ `speak_returns_promptly_via_spawn_on_macos` (asserts < 250ms for a 5-second Kazakh sentence), `second_speak_kills_previous_child_on_macos` (verifies PID change), `speak_empty_input_is_noop`. **Verified:** workspace **1094 passing** (+3 from new v5.0.5 tests) + 17 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 5.0.5 green; fmt + build clean. world_core: 3003 / 3245 / 30892 unchanged. **Roadmap (next):** v5.1.0 optional Piper backend; v5.2.0+ phoneme bank. Stripe ‚ÄĒ Kazakh school tutor (responsive multimodal output). | 1094 (+ 3 v5.0.5 non-blocking tests) |
| v5.0.0 | **Voice output transducer ‚ÄĒ adam speaks Kazakh.** First multimodal release. Pre-v5.0.0 every adam response was silent text; post-v5.0.0 the optional `--tts` flag activates a system-native voice synthesiser so adam **speaks** every response in addition to printing it. **Architectural framing:** TTS is a **peripheral output transducer** ‚ÄĒ not a kernel component. Dialog kernel produces the same Kazakh text as before; TTS layer just speaks that text via OS-native command (`say` on macOS, `espeak-ng` on Linux). | v4.97.0 | **Codex 2026-05-07 round-2 audit Bug 3 (P1) ‚ÄĒ REPL multi-line code-block accumulator. Round-2 audit fully closed (7 / 7 bugs).** Pre-fix: `adam_chat` read one line per turn, so multi-line ` ```rust ... ``` ` blocks had to be entered with `\n` escapes. Post-fix: when a line opens a fence that doesn't close on the same line, the REPL accumulates subsequent lines until the closing fence appears, then submits the assembled block as one turn. Inline blocks bypass the accumulator (v4.96.0 Bug 4 path); empty lines inside an open block are preserved (Rust functions can have blank separators); empty lines outside are skipped. **Touches:** [adam_chat.rs](../crates/adam-dialog/src/bin/adam_chat.rs) ‚ÄĒ new `absorb_line` state-machine helper + `count_fences` parity counter. **Regression tests:** 10 new binary unit tests covering parity invariant + open / body / close sequence + inline-block bypass + empty-line behaviour. **Smoke test:** end-to-end multi-line Rust block via stdin ‚Üí adam runs `cargo check` ‚Üí returns ¬ę–Ė–į—Ä–į–Ļ—Ā—č–∑!¬Ľ verdict. **Verified:** workspace **1036 passing** (+10 from new REPL accumulator tests) + 11 ignored slow integration; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency green; verify_release_version 4.97.0 green; fmt + build clean. world_core: 3003 / 3245 / 30892 unchanged. **Round-2 audit status:** all 7 bugs closed (1/2/4/6/7 in v4.96.0 + 5 in v4.96.5 + 3 in v4.97.0). **Roadmap (next):** open per user direction ‚ÄĒ adaptive difficulty, lesson-state dialog tree, or new book (Rustonomicon / Embedded Rust / Tokio Tutorial / Cargo Book). | v4.75.0 | **Paren-aware arithmetic ‚ÄĒ recursive-descent parser; lifts v4.74.5 paren-rejection guard** ‚ÄĒ Replaces v4.74.x flat token-based arithmetic evaluator with proper recursive-descent parser that respects parentheses and operator precedence. Closes v4.74.5 deferred case where ¬ęP=2*(a+b), a=5, b=3¬Ľ honestly refused (paren guard) ‚ÄĒ now computes 16 correctly. Pure deterministic; no NN. **Innovations:** recursive-descent parser in `discourse::try_evaluate_arithmetic` with standard grammar (expr = term (('+'|'-') term)*; term = factor (('*'|'/') factor)*; factor = '-' factor | '+' factor | '(' expr ')' | number). Handles operator precedence (√ó√∑ before +‚ąí), arbitrarily nested parens, leading unary minus/plus, negative numbers via factor recursion (-(-5) parses as 5), integer overflow via checked_* ops, division by zero ‚Üí None graceful. Kazakh-wrapper stripping from v4.74.0 preserved; kept-char set extended with `(` and `)`. | v4.74.5 | **Procedural formula-applier ‚ÄĒ ¬ęF=m*a, m=2, a=3 –Ī–ĺ–Ľ—Ā–į F “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į?¬Ľ** ‚ÄĒ Second procedural solver in v4.74.x series. | v4.74.0 | **First procedural solver ‚ÄĒ natural-Kazakh arithmetic wrapper + linear equation solver** ‚ÄĒ First step on the procedural-tutor roadmap. Per `project_kazakh_tutor_positioning`, project is Kazakh school tutor; Codex round-2 #1-priority gap was ¬ęno procedural tutor ‚ÄĒ solve_equation/check_answer/explain_steps refused¬Ľ. This release ships the simplest two solvers: arithmetic wrapped in natural Kazakh + 1-unknown linear equation. Both fully deterministic ‚ÄĒ no NN involved (per roadmap, NN integration scoped to v5+). **Bugs fixed:** ¬ę5+7*2 “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į?¬Ľ previously refused because `try_evaluate_arithmetic` cleaned string contained Cyrillic letters from ¬ę“õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į¬Ľ. ¬ę–ē–≥–Ķ—Ä x+2=5 –Ī–ĺ–Ľ—Ā–į, x “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į?¬Ľ previously refused because no equation solver existed. **Innovations:** (1) `discourse::try_evaluate_arithmetic` pre-extracts longest contiguous arithmetic substring (digits + ASCII operators) before evaluation ‚ÄĒ drops Kazakh wrapper words. (2) New `discourse::try_solve_linear_equation` ‚ÄĒ deterministic 1-unknown linear equation solver. Handles 7 forms: x = b (trivial), x op a = b, a op x = b for op ‚ąą {+, ‚ąí, √ó, √∑}. Detection: scans whitespace-separated tokens for one containing `=`; works inside any natural-Kazakh wrapper. Returns `(unknown, value)` tuple. Conservative: rejects multi-unknown, fractional, or non-integer-solution forms. (3) `Conversation::turn` integration: when arithmetic + Kazakh-word-math both fail BUT linear-equation solver succeeds, surfaces value via `__math_answer__` slot path (existing `math_answer` template family fires) plus `__math_unknown__` slot for variable name. **Verified test cases:** 5+7*2 “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į ‚Üí 19, 5+7*2 “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į –Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į–ī—č ‚Üí 19, x+2=5 ‚Üí 3, x*3=15 ‚Üí 5, 10-y=4 ‚Üí 6. **Acceptance:** 100-query battery diff vs v4.73.5 = 0 differences (zero regression); workspace 976 passing; clippy `-D warnings` green; check_metrics_currency.sh green (9/9); verify_release_version.sh 4.74.0 green; fmt + build clean. **Deferred:** quadratic/multi-unknown equations (need symbolic algebra); formula-applier (F=ma, m=2, a=3 –Ī–ĺ–Ľ—Ā–į F “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į?); `check_answer` intent; `explain_steps` intent; Codex round-2 bugs 3-8. **Strategic note:** `.0` minor not `.5` because adding new procedural capability is meaningful feature increment per `feedback_versioning_post_1_0`. v4.74.x will be pure deterministic procedural work; NN integration (disambiguator first) scoped to v5.0.0+. | v4.71.5 | **Live REPL audit fixes ‚ÄĒ loanword topic recognition + relation-predicate demotion** ‚ÄĒ Driven by 12-query REPL battery against v4.66.0+ educational stripe (8/12 queries surfaced correctly, 2 bugs identified). **Bug 1**: ¬ę–ź–Ĺ—ā–į—Ä–ļ—ā–ł–ī–į “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ –ľ–į—ā–Ķ—Ä–ł–ļ?¬Ľ fell to `unknown.clarify_no_topic` ‚ÄĒ root cause: noun_hint = None because Antarctic / continents / oceans / metaf–ĺ—Ä–į / acetone / etc. are FST-unknown loanwords and no topic marker (¬ę—ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č¬Ľ, ¬ę–ī–Ķ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ¬Ľ) was present, so `first_noun_root` had no candidates. **Bug 2**: ¬ę–ľ–Ķ—ā–į—Ą–ĺ—Ä–į –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ —ć–Ņ–ł—ā–Ķ—ā –Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č –ľ–į?¬Ľ misrouted to unrelated ¬ę—Ö–į–Ľ—č“õ —ā—č“ď—č–∑–ī—č“ď—č¬Ľ fact ‚ÄĒ root cause: –ľ–Ķ—ā–į—Ą–ĺ—Ä–į / —ć–Ņ–ł—ā–Ķ—ā not in FST lexicon; FST analyses ¬ę–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č¬Ľ (predicate adjective form) as a form of –Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā (noun = "connection") and `first_noun_root` returns it as the topic, ignoring the actual subjects. **Fixes:** **(1)** Demote `–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā` / `–Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č` to `NOT_A_TOPIC` ‚ÄĒ these are relational predicates surfaced by ¬ęX –Ņ–Ķ–Ĺ Y –Ī–į–Ļ–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č –ľ–į?¬Ľ queries, never the topic. **(2)** Extend `MULTIWORD_ENTITIES` with ~85 single-word loanword topics from the educational stripe: world geography (–į–Ĺ—ā–į—Ä–ļ—ā–ł–ī–į / –Ķ—É—Ä–į–∑–ł—Ź / –į—Ą—Ä–ł–ļ–į / –į–≤—Ā—ā—Ä–į–Ľ–ł—Ź / –ľ–Ķ—Ā–ĺ–Ņ–ĺ—ā–į–ľ–ł—Ź / —Ä–Ķ–Ĺ–Ķ—Ā—Ā–į–Ĺ—Ā), mathematics (–į–Ľ–≥–Ķ–Ī—Ä–į / –≥–Ķ–ĺ–ľ–Ķ—ā—Ä–ł—Ź / —ā—Ä–ł–≥–ĺ–Ĺ–ĺ–ľ–Ķ—ā—Ä–ł—Ź / –į–Ļ–Ĺ—č–ľ–į–Ľ—č / –ļ–ĺ–ĺ—Ä–ī–ł–Ĺ–į—ā–į / —Ą—É–Ĺ–ļ—Ü–ł—Ź / —ā–Ķ“£–ī–Ķ—É / —ā–Ķ“£—Ā—Ė–∑–ī—Ė–ļ / –ī–ł—Ā–ļ—Ä–ł–ľ–ł–Ĺ–į–Ĺ—ā), physics (–ľ–Ķ—Ö–į–Ĺ–ł–ļ–į / –ļ–ł–Ĺ–Ķ–ľ–į—ā–ł–ļ–į / –ī–ł–Ĺ–į–ľ–ł–ļ–į / —Ā—ā–į—ā–ł–ļ–į / —ā–Ķ—Ä–ľ–ĺ–ī–ł–Ĺ–į–ľ–ł–ļ–į / —ć–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā—Ä–ĺ–ī–ł–Ĺ–į–ľ–ł–ļ–į / –ĺ–Ņ—ā–ł–ļ–į / –≥—Ä–į–≤–ł—ā–į—Ü–ł—Ź / —ā–Ķ–ľ–Ņ–Ķ—Ä–į—ā—É—Ä–į / —ć–Ĺ–Ķ—Ä–≥–ł—Ź / –ł–ľ–Ņ—É–Ľ—Ć—Ā / –ł–Ĺ–Ķ—Ä—Ü–ł—Ź / –ļ–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ĺ—Ā–į—ā–ĺ—Ä), chemistry atoms+elements+organics+polymers (~40 entries), literature literary devices (–ľ–Ķ—ā–į—Ą–ĺ—Ä–į / —ć–Ņ–ł—ā–Ķ—ā / —ā–Ķ“£–Ķ—É / –≥–ł–Ņ–Ķ—Ä–Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į / –ļ–Ķ–Ļ—Ė–Ņ—ā–Ķ—É / –į–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–≥–ĺ—Ä–ł—Ź / –į—Ā—Ā–ĺ–Ĺ–į–Ĺ—Ā / –į–Ľ–Ľ–ł—ā–Ķ—Ä–į—Ü–ł—Ź), medicine concepts (–ľ–Ķ–ī–ł—Ü–ł–Ĺ–į / –į–Ĺ–į—ā–ĺ–ľ–ł—Ź / —Ą–ł–∑–ł–ĺ–Ľ–ĺ–≥–ł—Ź / —Ā–ł–ľ–Ņ—ā–ĺ–ľ / –ī–ł–į–≥–Ĺ–ĺ–∑ / –Ņ—Ä–ĺ—Ą–ł–Ľ–į–ļ—ā–ł–ļ–į / –ł–ľ–ľ—É–Ĺ–ł—ā–Ķ—ā / –≤–į–ļ—Ü–ł–Ĺ–į / –į–Ĺ—ā–ł–Ī–ł–ĺ—ā–ł–ļ / –≤–ł—Ä—É—Ā / –Ī–į–ļ—ā–Ķ—Ä–ł—Ź). **(3)** Word-boundary token match for single-token entries ‚ÄĒ `multiword_entity_hint` first-pass now uses `tokens.iter().any(|t| t == entity)` for single-word entries (preserves substring match for multi-word). | v4.55.5 | **Architecture rename: NLM ‚Üí ARK (Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel)** ‚ÄĒ driven by user decision (2026-05-05). The architecture name ¬ęNLM¬Ľ (Nano Language Model) bucketed adam with the LLM family. **ARK** = Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel names what adam actually is ‚ÄĒ agglutinative morphology + curated knowledge graph + forward-chaining reasoner + tiny trained selection weights, packaged as a system-runtime not a probabilistic estimator. **Naming choice (history):** user rejected AGM (Agglutinative Grammar Model ‚ÄĒ ¬ęGrammar¬Ľ triggered school-grammar associations) and CALM (Controlled Agglutinative Language Model ‚ÄĒ ¬ęControlled¬Ľ was redundant since ¬ęAgglutinative¬Ľ already implies discipline by morphological nature). User-accepted ARK because all three letters are load-bearing: A=morphological algebra (already deterministic per nature), R=reasoning (the actual differentiator vs LLM), K=kernel (system-runtime, vs ¬ęModel¬Ľ = probabilistic estimator; aligns with existing `adam-kernel` crate). **(1)** `SystemIdentity::canonical()` in `crates/adam-dialog/src/system_identity.rs` ‚ÄĒ `full_name = "Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel"`, `abbreviation = "ARK"`; doc-comment references the v4.55.5 rename; unit test `canonical_identity_carries_all_required_fields` updated. **(2)** Latin-token whitelist in `crates/adam-dialog/src/quality.rs::is_allowed_latin_token` extended with `Agglutinative` / `Reasoning` / `Kernel` / `ARK`. Legacy tokens (`Nano`, `Language`, `Model`, `NLM`) kept on the whitelist for backwards compat with historical CHANGELOG entries + curated facts. **(3)** Templates updated in `data/dialog/templates/v1.toml`: `greeting.intro_proposal` line 74 ¬ę–ł”ô, ”ô—Ä–ł–Ĺ–Ķ. –ú–Ķ–Ĺ ‚ÄĒ “õ–į–∑–į“õ—ą–į —Ā”©–Ļ–Ľ–Ķ—Ā—É–≥–Ķ –į—Ä–Ĺ–į–Ľ“ď–į–Ĺ **ARK**, –į—ā—č–ľ –į–ī–į–ľ.¬Ľ; `ask_about_system` line 206 ¬ę**ARK** ‚ÄĒ Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel, –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ –į–ī–į–ľ –į—ā—ā—č “õ–į–∑–į“õ—ą–į —ā—Ė–Ľ–ī—Ė–ļ –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ć–ľ—Ė–Ĺ¬Ľ. **(4)** 3 new world_core entries in `data/world_core/adam_self.jsonl` (`adam_self_040‚Ä¶042`): `adam IsA ARK` (identity bridge); `ARK IsA –ī–Ķ—ā–Ķ—Ä–ľ–ł–Ĺ–ł—Ä–Ľ–Ķ–Ĺ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ –∂“Į–Ļ–Ķ` (frames as deterministic system, not probabilistic LM); `ARK IsA –į—Ä—Ö–ł—ā–Ķ–ļ—ā—É—Ä–į –į—ā–į—É—č` (names this as architecture-class label). **(5)** 2 new MULTIWORD_ENTITIES in `crates/adam-dialog/src/topic_extraction.rs` (¬ę–į—Ä—Ö–ł—ā–Ķ–ļ—ā—É—Ä–į –į—ā–į—É—č¬Ľ, ¬ę–ī–Ķ—ā–Ķ—Ä–ľ–ł–Ĺ–ł—Ä–Ľ–Ķ–Ĺ–≥–Ķ–Ĺ –∂“Į–Ļ–Ķ¬Ľ) so topic extractor surfaces them as a unit. **(6)** Eval data updated: `data/eval/cognitive_dialog_dataset.json` `ask_about_system_general_aspect_surfaces_full_name` expects `agglutinative reasoning kernel` OR `ark`; `data/eval/repl_dialogs.json` `ask_about_system_general` accepts ARK / Agglutinative Reasoning Kernel; `data/eval/live_holdout_2026_05_01.json` `identity_who_are_you` accepts `ark` / `agglutinative reasoning kernel`. **(7)** README ‚ÄĒ new ¬ęArchitecture name ‚ÄĒ ARK¬Ľ section above the Engineering thesis, documenting four-pillar definition + rationale + renaming context. Bigram match: when a converb token is found AND the next token starts with ¬ę–∂–į—ā—č—Ä¬Ľ (covers ¬ę–∂–į—ā—č—Ä–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ 1sg / ¬ę–∂–į—ā—č—Ä–ľ—č–∑¬Ľ 1pl), treat the converb as the verb position; walk back to extract object. **(2)** Two new activity-verb roots ‚ÄĒ ¬ę–ī–į–ľ—č—ā—É¬Ľ (develop) + ¬ę“õ“Ī—Ä—É¬Ľ (build/establish); 4 surface forms added to `ACTIVITY_VERBS`: –ī–į–ľ—č—ā–į–ľ—č–Ĺ / “õ“Ī—Ä–į–ľ—č–Ĺ (finite) + –ī–į–ľ—č—ā–į—ā—č–Ĺ / “õ“Ī—Ä–į—ā—č–Ĺ (participle). **(3)** `detect_occupation_in_compound(input, lexicon)` ‚ÄĒ new pure function in `semantics.rs`. Mirrors `detect_activity_in_compound`. Tokenises lowered input; calls `strip_copula_and_lookup_noun` against the lexicon for the priority path; falls back to a 15-entry fixed-table lookup when no lexicon is provided. Returns `Some(Some(root))` when a noun + 1sg-copula form is identifiable. **(4)** `Conversation::turn` secondary occupation scan ‚ÄĒ runs after primary intent absorption + activity scan. When primary intent is NOT `StatementOfOccupation` AND the session doesn't already have an `occupation` slot, calls `detect_occupation_in_compound`. Captures occupation into session + belief graph. Lets a single utterance like ¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –į—ā—č–ľ X, –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ Y-–ľ—č–Ĺ ...¬Ľ populate `name` + `occupation` + `activity` slots in one turn. **(5)** AskActivity self-recall extended ‚ÄĒ `detect_ask_activity` treats any ¬ę–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£¬Ľ + activity-participle stem as 1sg self-recall. New stems: –ī–į–ľ—č—ā–į—ā—č–Ĺ / ”ô–∑—Ė—Ä–Ľ–Ķ–Ļ—ā—Ė–Ĺ / –∂–į—Ā–į–Ļ—ā—č–Ĺ / –∂–į–∑–į—ā—č–Ĺ / –∑–Ķ—Ä—ā—ā–Ķ–Ļ—ā—Ė–Ĺ / “õ“Ī—Ä–į—Ā—ā—č—Ä–į—ā—č–Ĺ. Pre-v4.52.0 only ¬ę—Ė—Ā—ā–Ķ–Ļ—ā—Ė–Ĺ¬Ľ was matched. **(6)** Demonstrative math anaphora ¬ę–Ī“Ī–Ľ –Ĺ”ô—ā–ł–∂–Ķ¬Ľ ‚ÄĒ `Conversation::turn` math anaphora resolver gains a third anaphora family alongside ¬ę–į–Ľ–ī—č“£“ď—č¬Ľ / ¬ę—Ā–ĺ“£“ď—č¬Ľ: ¬ę–Ī“Ī–Ľ (–Ķ—Ā–Ķ–Ņ—ā–Ķ—É )?–Ĺ”ô—ā–ł–∂–Ķ¬Ľ with full case-suffix preservation (Acc / Dat). **Live REPL replay:** ¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –į—ā—č–ľ –Ē”ô—É–Ľ–Ķ—ā, –ľ–Ķ–Ĺ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—ą—č–ľ—č–Ĺ –∂”ô–Ĺ–Ķ ”©–∑—Ė–ľ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –∂–į—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č –ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ė–ľ–ī—Ė –∂–į—Ā–į–Ņ –∂–į—ā—č—Ä–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ ‚Üí all three slots captured (was name-only); ¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –Ĺ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė –ī–į–ľ—č—ā–į—ā—č–Ĺ—č–ľ –Ķ—Ā—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī–Ķ –ľ–Ķ?¬Ľ ‚Üí "–Ė–į—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č –ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ ‚ÄĒ —Ā—Ė–∑–ī—Ė“£ “õ–į–∑—Ė—Ä–≥—Ė —Ė—Ā—Ė“£—Ė–∑ –ī–Ķ–Ņ –∂–į–ī—č–ľ–į —ā“Į—Ā—Ė—Ä–ī—Ė–ľ" (was clarify); ¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –ľ–į–ľ–į–Ĺ–ī—č“ď—č–ľ “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?¬Ľ ‚Üí "–ú–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –Ī—Ė–Ľ—É—Ė–ľ—ą–Ķ, –ľ–į–ľ–į–Ĺ–ī—č“ď—č“£—č–∑ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—ą—č" (was no-slot fallback); ¬ę–ē–Ĺ–ī—Ė –Ī“Ī–Ľ –Ĺ”ô—ā–ł–∂–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė 4-–ļ–Ķ –Ī”©–Ľ—Ė“£—Ė–∑¬Ľ ‚Üí 6 (was math_refusal). **Verification:** Workspace 969 passing unchanged; adam-dialog lib 301; live REPL 4/4 session-5 scenarios verified; foundation unchanged 2089/2349/46/27175; fmt + build clean. | v4.51.0 | **User-activity slot extraction (Stage A architectural addition)** ‚ÄĒ closes the v4.50.5 carry-forward. Pre-v4.51.0 a compound input ¬ę–ú–Ķ–Ĺ –Ī–į“ď–ī–į—Ä–Ľ–į–ľ–į—ą—č–ľ—č–Ĺ –∂”ô–Ĺ–Ķ –∂–į—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č –ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā ”ô–∑—Ė—Ä–Ľ–Ķ–Ļ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ¬Ľ captured only the occupation; v4.51.0 captures both via a secondary compound-clause scan. **(1)** `Intent::StatementOfActivity { activity: Option<String> }` + `Intent::AskActivity` new variants. `IntentKind` companions added (29 ‚Üí **31 intents**). **(2)** `detect_statement_of_activity(tokens, joined)` pure-function detector ‚ÄĒ recognizes 6 activity-verb stems (1sg-conjugated): ”ô–∑—Ė—Ä–Ľ–Ķ–Ļ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ / –∂–į—Ā–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ / –∂–į–∑–į–ľ—č–Ĺ / –∑–Ķ—Ä—ā—ā–Ķ–Ļ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ / –į–Ļ–Ĺ–į–Ľ—č—Ā–į–ľ—č–Ĺ / “õ“Ī—Ä–į—Ā—ā—č—Ä–į–ľ—č–Ĺ. Walks backwards from verb position to extract noun phrase, stops at clause boundaries (¬ę–∂”ô–Ĺ–Ķ¬Ľ, ¬ę–į–Ľ¬Ľ, ¬ę—Ā–ĺ–ī–į–Ĺ¬Ľ, ¬ę–Ī—Ė—Ä–į“õ¬Ľ, ¬ę—Ā–ĺ–Ĺ–ī—č“õ—ā–į–Ĺ¬Ľ, ¬ę–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ¬Ľ, ¬ę–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£¬Ľ) or commas. Strips Accusative (¬ę-–ī—č/-–ī—Ė/-–Ĺ—č/-–Ĺ—Ė/-—ā—č/-—ā—Ė¬Ľ) / Comitative (¬ę-–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ/-–Ņ–Ķ–Ĺ/-–Ī–Ķ–Ĺ¬Ľ) case suffixes from the head noun. | v4.50.5 | **Transcript-driven regression fixes ‚ÄĒ math truncation + respectful address + math vocabulary** ‚ÄĒ driven by 2026-05-04 user dialog test session 3. Three concrete gaps closed plus one knowledge addition. **(1)** Truncated integer division in `try_evaluate_arithmetic` ‚ÄĒ pre-v4.50.5 returned None for non-integer (`7/2`); v4.50.5 truncates to `Some(3)`. Division by zero stays None. **(2)** Same fix in `try_evaluate_kazakh_word_math` ‚ÄĒ ¬ę–Ė–Ķ—ā—Ė–Ĺ—Ė –Ķ–ļ—Ė–≥–Ķ –Ī”©–Ľ¬Ľ now `Some(3)`. Multi-clause word-form queries with non-integer intermediates now compute through. **(3)** Respect-form-by-default `statement_of_name` template family ‚ÄĒ replaced v4.18.0 4-template family (3 literal-name + 1 respect-aware) with new 4-template family where 3 of 4 gate on `{name_respect_distinct}`. | v4.45.5 | **Stage B bundle 2 ‚ÄĒ pairwise margin-perceptron training pipeline** ‚ÄĒ Stage B continues. v4.45.0 shipped the foundation (`SelectionWeights` + `extract_features` + `score` + `select_top`). v4.45.5 ships the training algorithm: pairwise margin perceptron that takes a list of gold `(positive, negative)` candidate pairs and tunes a `SelectionWeights` table until every pair satisfies `score(positive) ‚Č• score(negative) + margin` (or `max_epochs` elapse). Pure function, deterministic per `(initial, pairs, config)`. **Architectural fit:** discrete (no gradient graph, no library deps), inspectable (still ~28 bytes after training), deterministic (no random sampling, no SGD batching variance). Satisfies the thesis constraint ¬ęweights/learning OK if discrete, inspectable, cheap; reject only LLM internals¬Ľ. **(1)** `TrainingPair` struct ‚ÄĒ labelled gold pair (positive vs negative candidate). **(2)** `TrainingConfig` ‚ÄĒ three hyperparameters (`learning_rate / margin / max_epochs`); `default_v0` hand-tuned for v0 feature scale. **(3)** `TrainingStats` ‚ÄĒ `epochs_run / final_violations / converged` reporting. **(4)** `train_perceptron(initial, pairs, config) -> (SelectionWeights, TrainingStats)` ‚ÄĒ pure loop; per-epoch iterates pairs; failing pairs trigger update by `lr √ó (pos_feature - neg_feature)` per weight component; early-exit on zero violations. **(5)** Re-exports in lib.rs. **(6)** 11 new unit tests verify convergence on linearly-separable data, determinism, no-op when pre-converged, max-epoch reporting, empty-pair handling, single-dimension signal pickup (recency / confidence), zero-lr no-progress, multi-signal convergence within budget, post-training rank correctness, epoch-count reporting, default-config stability. **(7)** NOT YET in v4.45.5 ‚ÄĒ real training data pipeline from canonical evals + REPL transcripts, audit-only wiring (compute selection scores at SearchGraph result point + log disagreement), production routing replacement of heuristic top-1 ranker. **Stage B status:** v4.45.0 ‚ÄĒ bundle 1 ‚ÄĒ foundation ‚úď; v4.45.5 ‚ÄĒ bundle 2 ‚ÄĒ training pipeline ‚úď; v4.46.0+ ‚ÄĒ bundle 3 ‚ÄĒ real training data + audit-only wiring; v4.50.0 (target) ‚ÄĒ bundle 4 ‚ÄĒ trained-weights replacement of heuristic ranker. **Verification:** Workspace **936 passing** (was 925; +11 training tests); adam-dialog lib **269 passing** (+11); selection module 24/24 (13 v4.45.0 + 11 v4.45.5); live REPL byte-identical to v4.45.0 (no production wiring yet); foundation unchanged 2086/2346/46/27163; fmt + check clean. | v4.15.0 | **First compositional ML layer: P(suffix_chain) priors + offline training pass** ‚ÄĒ first minor in the v4.15+ compositional-ML arc. The Kazakh agglutinative grammar IS typed function composition (`root + suffix^n`). Pre-v4.15.0 the FST analyser had no distributional signal over which chains are actually common in Kazakh. v4.15.0 adds it as a frozen prior. **Infrastructure-only release**: the prior is loaded but not yet integrated into runtime decision-making ‚ÄĒ splitting the architectural addition from the behaviour change keeps both reversible. **Architectural addition:** new module `crates/adam-kernel-fst/src/suffix_priors.rs` (~280 lines + 8 tests). `struct SuffixPriors { version, trained_on_tokens, chain_log_prob }`. `from_counts` uses add-one Laplace smoothing; `score_noun`/`score_verb` are single hashmap probes. Unseen chains return `min_observed - ln(2)` so they rank strictly below the rarest observed chain. Schema-versioned (v1 at v4.15.0); loader rejects mismatched versions. **Training pass:** new binary `crates/adam-corpus/src/bin/train_suffix_priors.rs`. Walks `data/curated/*.json` packs, FST-analyses each token, attributes uniform `1/N` weight to each candidate (unbiased given no labels), writes `data/retrieval/suffix_chain_priors.json` deterministically (sorted keys, byte-stable across runs). Why uniform attribution: first-parse weighting would make the prior a circular reflection of existing tie-breaking; uniform attribution captures which chains *appear at all* in real Kazakh text. Per user's directive (`project_v4_direction`): Predictable (no embeddings/SGD), Cheap (~5min training, hashmap probe at runtime), Safe (only ranks existing parses, never invents), Foundation (preserves `–ļ–ĺ—Ä–Ķ–Ĺ—Ć + —Ą—É–Ĺ–ļ—Ü–ł—Ź^n`, version-bump path built in). Pipeline: 1 new module + 1 new binary + 1 frozen artifact + new dep edge `adam-corpus ‚Üí adam-kernel-fst`. **Cadence: minor.** Stripe (4) ‚ÄĒ compositional ML ‚ÄĒ opens. Next: v4.15.5 (runtime integration as tiebreaker), v4.16.0 (context-aware priors `P(chain | preceding_chain)`). | 793 (+8 suffix_priors unit tests) |

| v4.13.0 | **Sentence-decomposition foundation + DialogContext multi-turn topic memory + closed-class hygiene** ‚ÄĒ second minor in the v4.12+ humanness arc. | v4.12.0 | **Humanness milestone: question-shape classifier + Implementation aspect + causal-reasoning routing + backtick carve-out for user output** ‚ÄĒ first minor in the v4.12+ humanness research arc. Stripe (1) ‚ÄĒ "answer-by-the-point" ‚ÄĒ closed in v4.11.5/.6/.7 across all 38 world_core domains; v4.12.0 opens stripe (2) ‚ÄĒ "human-like reasoning" ‚ÄĒ by giving the planner an analytical signal it never had: the **form** of the user's question, independent of topic. **Architectural addition:** new `crates/adam-dialog/src/question_shape.rs` module with `QuestionShape` enum (5 variants: Definition, Causal, YesNoCheck, Listing, Comparison) + pure surface-level `detect(input)`; new `Intent::Unknown.question_shape: Option<QuestionShape>` field populated at top of `interpret_text_with_lexicon`; preserved across `verifier::strip_evidence`. **(1)** New `SystemAspect::Implementation` variant + detector + template family `ask_about_system.implementation` + new `SystemIdentity::implementation_summary` field (mentions `Rust`, crate stack, FST + rule-based architecture, `macOS`/`Linux`). | v4.7.16 | **Rust Book Chapter 16 (“ö–ĺ—Ä“õ—č–Ĺ—č—ą—Ā—č–∑ “õ–į—ā–į—Ä–Ľ–į—Ā –ĺ—Ä—č–Ĺ–ī–į—É) translated, in pack (¬ę–≥–Ľ–į–≤–į = –Ņ–į—ā—á¬Ľ cadence on the v4.7.x minor)** ‚ÄĒ sixteenth chapter under user-confirmed cadence. | v4.6.20 | **Bundle of 5 more innovations (20 total cumulative on the v4.6.x minor): reflexive identity question + adj+noun compound noun-hint + `SelfComparison` aspect + preamble stripper + `UserAcknowledgement` intent** ‚ÄĒ real-REPL 2026-04-29 (fifth transcript) surfaced 5 distinct defects sharing one theme: greedy noun-hint extraction on long multi-clause sentences grabbed closed-class adverbs or modifier-stripped head nouns and surfaced random poetry/contract quotes. **(1)** `detect_ask_about_system` extended for reflexive identity questions ¬ę”®–∑—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė –ļ—Ė–ľ –ī–Ķ–Ņ —Ā–į–Ĺ–į–Ļ—Ā—č–∑?¬Ľ / ¬ę”®–∑—Ė“£–ī—Ė “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ —ā–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā—č—Ä–į—Ā—č“£?¬Ľ (marker: `”©–∑—Ė“£–ī—Ė / ”©–∑—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė` + 2nd-person verb), routed to `SystemAspect::General`. **(2)** New `discourse::find_adj_noun_compound` returns the longest matching closed-list compound (`–ľ–į—ą–ł–Ĺ–į–Ľ—č“õ –ĺ“õ—č—ā—É`, `–∂–į—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č –ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā`, `—ā–į–Ī–ł“ď–ł —ā—Ė–Ľ`, `—ā–Ķ—Ä–Ķ“£ –ĺ“õ—č—ā—É`, `–Ĺ–Ķ–Ļ—Ä–ĺ–Ĺ–ī—č“õ –∂–Ķ–Ľ—Ė` ‚Ä¶); wired as the FIRST strategy in `best_noun_hint`. **(3)** New 9th `SystemAspect::SelfComparison` + `system_self_comparison` slot + `ask_about_system.self_comparison` template. Detector pairs comparison marker (`–į—Ä—ā—č“õ/–∂–į“õ—Ā—č—Ä–į“õ/–ĺ–∑–į—Ā—č“£`) with addressee anchor incl. `-—Ā—č“£/-—Ā—č–∑` ability suffix. Honest trade-off framing (narrow KZ-only competence with strong invariants vs. broad LLM coverage), not superiority claim. Closes ¬ę–Ď–į—Ā“õ–į –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ć–ī–Ķ—Ä–ī–Ķ–Ĺ –Ĺ–Ķ—Ā—Ė–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ –į—Ä—ā—č“õ—Ā—č–∑?¬Ľ, ¬ę“ö–ĺ–Ľ–ī–į–Ĺ—č—Ā—ā–į“ď—č –ľ–ĺ–ī–Ķ–Ľ—Ć–ī–Ķ—Ä–ī–Ķ–Ĺ “õ–į–Ľ–į–Ļ –∂–į“õ—Ā—č—Ä–į“õ –Ī–ĺ–Ľ–į –į–Ľ–į—Ā—č–∑?¬Ľ. **(4)** New `discourse::strip_preamble` runs at top of `Conversation::turn_with_trace` BEFORE FST parsing. | v4.5.0 | **`Case::LocativeAttributive` FST morphotactics rule** ‚ÄĒ third v4.x minor. | v4.4.13 | **Lexicon hygiene patch: multi-POS homonym dedup + missing core nouns + `best_noun_hint` reorder** ‚ÄĒ closes both v4.4.12 carry-forward defects. **(1)** Pre-v4.4.13 `Lexicon::load` deduplicated by surface root via `HashMap<String, RootEntry>`, so multi-POS homonyms like `—ā–į—É` (verb_tau + noun_apt_tau) silently lost one reading and the FST analyser saw only the wrong POS. Fix: separate `entries_ordered` (full union of curated + apertium files, dedup only by `id + part_of_speech` to handle exact-copy entries) from `by_surface` (lossy single-POS lookup unchanged). The FST analyser iterates `entries_ordered` and now produces multi-POS analyses. **(2)** Three core nouns absent from the lexicon entirely ‚ÄĒ `—Ā—É` (water), `–ĺ—ā` (fire), `–Ķ—Ä` (saddle / man-as-hero). Added to `data/tokenizer/segmentation_roots.json`. **(3)** Knock-on: v4.4.13's lexicon-dedup fix unblocked `—ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä ‚Üí —ā–į—É +Plural` parsing, which made `first_noun_root` start returning `—ā–į—É` and masked the locative-attributive signal on questions like `“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?`. Reordered `best_noun_hint` to run `locative_attributive_hint` immediately after `topic_marker_hint` (before `multiword_entity_hint` / `first_noun_root`) ‚ÄĒ the `-–ī–į“ď—č` morpheme is a strong topic-narrowing signal semantically equivalent to a `—ā—É—Ä–į–Ľ—č` marker. All 5 listing-style questions now answer correctly with both locative (`“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä –Ī–į—Ä?`) and locative-attributive (`“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?`) phrasings. 2 new e2e regressions (multi-POS homonym lock + core-noun lock) + 3 REPL replay dialogs (rivers / lakes / deserts via locative-attributive). | v4.4.12 | **Locative-attributive `-–ī–į“ď—č / -–ī–Ķ–≥—Ė / -—ā–į“ď—č / -—ā–Ķ–≥—Ė` suffix recovery** ‚ÄĒ closes the v4.4.11 carry-forward where `“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–ī–į“ď—č —ā–į—É–Ľ–į—Ä “õ–į–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ?` fell through to the generic refusal because the FST morphotactics encodes the 7 canonical cases but not the locative-attributive derivation (`-“ď—č / -–≥—Ė / -“õ—č / -–ļ—Ė` on a locative-cased stem). New string-level fallback `locative_attributive_hint` in `crates/adam-dialog/src/semantics.rs` scans whitespace-separated tokens, finds those ending in one of the four allomorphs, strips the 4-char tail, returns the first stem (‚Č• 3 codepoints, not in NOT_A_TOPIC). Wired into `best_noun_hint` after `first_noun_root` ‚ÄĒ only fires when FST + earlier strategies recovered nothing. Conservative by design ‚ÄĒ no lexicon lookup, 3-codepoint minimum filters obvious noise. 2 new e2e regressions (kazakhstan + almaty stems) + 1 cognitive scenario + 1 REPL replay dialog through the full retrieval path. | v4.4.5 | **Real-dialog adequacy fixes: CheckContradiction renderer + AskAge self-recall** ‚ÄĒ Codex external review (2026-04-27 live REPL) caught two v4.4.0 defects the internal suite missed. **(1)** `Action::CheckContradiction` rendered as a confirmation: action layer correctly chose CheckContradiction after `–ź—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ–į/–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č`, but the planner kept keying on `intent_key(StatementOfLocation) = "statement_of_location"` and emitted ¬ę–ź–Ľ–ľ–į—ā—č–ī–į –Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£—Ė–∑–ī—Ė –Ķ—Ā—ā–Ķ —Ā–į“õ—ā–į–Ļ–ľ—č–Ĺ¬Ľ, committing to one of the contested values. v4.4.0's dismiss/cap escape hatches were thus answering a question the user never saw asked. Fix: new `check_contradiction` template family (4 KZ variants of `{old_value}-–ī–į –ľ–į, ”ô–Ľ–ī–Ķ {new_value}-–ī–į –ľ–į?`) + new `__check_contradiction__` marker slot set in `Conversation::turn_with_trace` whenever `action_plan.action == CheckContradiction`; planner gets a third override branch parallel to v4.4.0's `__dismiss_contradiction__`. Conflict slots populated whenever either epistemic = Conflicted OR action = CheckContradiction. **(2)** `–ľ–Ķ–Ĺ—Ė“£ –∂–į—Ā—č–ľ “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į?` misclassified as `StatementOfAge { years: None }` (reply happened to surface 40 only because `statement_of_age` interpolates session.age). Root cause: `detect_statement_of_age` keyed on substring `–∂–į—Ā—č–ľ` and ran BEFORE `detect_ask_age`; ask-age only checked 2nd-person `–∂–į—Ā—č“£/–∂–į—Ā—č“£—č–∑`. Fix: `detect_ask_age` accepts 1sg `–∂–į—Ā—č–ľ + “õ–į–Ĺ—ą–į/–Ĺ–Ķ—ą–Ķ` + `detect_statement_of_age` returns None on question particles + reordered dispatch. Cognitive baseline: **52/52 ‚Üí 54/54 canonical** (+1 in `contradiction_recovery`, +1 in `direct_answer`). Tests: 678‚Üí680 (+2 e2e). Why patch: small, focused renderer + detector fixes ‚ÄĒ no new architectural layer, no new `Action` variant | 680 (+2 tests) |
| v4.4.0 | **Belief-poisoning recovery: `Action::DismissContradiction` + contradiction-priority cap (Phase 2 Track C)** ‚ÄĒ closes the post-v4.3.2 "no clean exit" failure mode where `BeliefState.contradictions` non-empty for *any* reason (real conflict, transient typo, parse glitch) clamped every subsequent `ActionPlanner.plan(...)` step 1 to `CheckContradiction` with no escape. Two complementary hatches: **(1) explicit user-initiated dismissal** ‚ÄĒ new `BeliefState::dismiss_contradiction(subject, predicate)` (symmetric to v4.1.0 `resolve_contradiction`) marks both contested facts `FactStatus::Superseded` + drops `BeliefConflict` + clears `ContradictionToResolve` pending; new `Conversation::try_dismiss_pending_contradiction(input)` fires only when contradictions non-empty AND input matches one of 9 KZ triggers (`–Ķ–ļ–Ķ—É—Ė –ī–Ķ –∂–ĺ“õ`, `–Ķ–ļ–Ķ—É—Ė –ī–Ķ –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā`, `–Ķ—ą“õ–į–Ļ—Ā—č—Ā—č –ī“Ī—Ä—č—Ā –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā`, `–Ī—Ė–Ľ–ľ–Ķ–Ļ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ`, `”©—ā–ļ—Ė–∑—Ė–Ņ –∂—Ė–Ī–Ķ—Ä`, `–ľ–į“£—č–∑–ī—č –Ķ–ľ–Ķ—Ā`, `–∂–į–ī—ā–į–Ĺ ”©—ą—Ė—Ä`, `“Ī–ľ—č—ā`, `–į–Ľ–į—Ā—ā–į—ā`); runs *before* `try_resolve_pending_contradiction` so "–Ī—Ė–Ľ–ľ–Ķ–Ļ–ľ—Ė–Ĺ" doesn't accidentally pick a candidate; absorption is skipped on a hit; planner short-circuited with direct `ActionPlan::new(Action::DismissContradiction, OutputKind::SocialPleasantry, ...)`; new `__dismiss_contradiction__` marker slot routes planner to dedicated `dismiss_contradiction` template family with 4 KZ variants; new `Action::DismissContradiction` variant (8‚Üí9), `Verifier` non-evidence-required + `OutputKind::SocialPleasantry`, `UncertaintyPolicy ‚Üí EpistemicStatus::Certain`. **(2) implicit time-bounded priority cap** ‚ÄĒ new `ActionPlanner::CONTRADICTION_PRIORITY_TURNS = 3` const + new `plan_with_turn(intent, belief, task, current_turn)` API (legacy `plan(...)` still wraps `plan_inner(..., None)` for callers without turn id); `Conversation::turn_with_trace` now passes `self.turn_counter`; step 1 of `plan_inner` checks `current_turn.saturating_sub(detected_at_turn) < K` instead of "any contradiction dominates forever," so a conflict logged at turn `T` dominates `T`/`T+1`/`T+2` and falls through on `T+3`; the conflict stays in `belief.contradictions` for audit, only planner priority changes. **Tests**: 3 unit tests for `dismiss_contradiction` (supersedes-all / no-op when empty / slot stays writable), 3 e2e regressions (`dismiss_contradiction_clears_both_cities_on_neither_reply`, `dismiss_contradiction_handles_dont_know_phrasing`, `contradiction_priority_cap_lets_user_move_on`), 2 new cognitive scenarios in new `contradiction_recovery` category. Cognitive baseline: **50/50 ‚Üí 52/52 canonical** (+1 category, +2 scenarios). Why minor: symmetric Belief op + planner contract change + new action variant + new template family ‚ÄĒ kernel-signature feature, not housekeeping | 678 (+6 tests net) |

| v4.3.2 | **Critical fix: phantom-city false positive + intelligence roadmap** ‚ÄĒ real test dialog (2026-04-26) showed the dialog locked into permanent CheckContradiction after a benign AI-modeling profession statement. Root cause: `token_mentions_generic_place` used `token.contains(stem)`; the 2-letter stem `–Ķ–Ľ` is a substring of `–ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā`, so `recover_named_place_before_generic_location` promoted `–∂–į—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č` to a city, the belief layer logged `(USER, city, –Ė–į—Ā–į–Ĺ–ī—č)` against `(USER, city, –ź—ā—č—Ä–į—É)`, planner blocked every subsequent topic. Fix: switch substring ‚Üí prefix match (`token.starts_with(stem)`) for both `token_mentions_generic_place` and `token_mentions_geo_descriptor`. Captures every real Kazakh word formation (`“õ–į–Ľ–į–ī–į`, `–į—É—č–Ľ–ī–į–Ĺ`, `–Ķ–Ľ–ī–Ķ`) without false positives on intra-word substrings (`–ł–Ĺ—ā–Ķ–Ľ–Ľ–Ķ–ļ—ā`, `–ļ–Ķ–Ľ–ī—Ė–ľ`, `–Ī–Ķ–Ľ–≥—Ė`). Cognitive baseline: 41/41 ‚Üí **42/42 canonical**. 656 tests (+1 end-to-end regression `jasandi_intellekt_does_not_break_dialog_with_false_city`, +1 cognitive `occupation_with_intellekt_does_not_create_phantom_city`). Same dialog test surfaced 3 other deficits documented in new `docs/intelligence_roadmap.md` (self/other intent distinction, belief-poisoning recovery, knowledge-breadth via SearchGraph routing) ‚ÄĒ Phase 1‚Äď4 program for v4.3.x ‚Üí v4.7.x | 656 (+1 test) |

| **v4.2.0** | **Tools-as-execution endgame ‚ÄĒ second v4.x minor (retire `inject_*`)** ‚ÄĒ closes the arc started in v4.0.37 (Tool layer substrate) ‚Üí v4.0.38 (audit-mode wiring) ‚Üí v4.1.1 (retrieval) ‚Üí v4.1.2 (reasoning) ‚Üí v4.1.5 (belief). v4.2.0 inverts the control structure: `inject_*` framing is gone; `turn_with_trace` builds `Vec<ToolCall>` via `tool_plan_for_turn(intent, parses)`, dispatches all in one map, folds results back via `apply_tool_results(intent, results, lexicon)`. | v4.1.5 | **Tools as execution, step 3 (belief lookup) ‚ÄĒ closes the triplet** ‚ÄĒ third v4.1.x patch (jumped .2 ‚Üí .5 to reflect milestone significance per the contribution-driven versioning rule). `ActionPlanner::belief_direct_answer` was the last of the three injection points still bypassing the tool layer; v4.1.5 routes it through `Tool::dispatch(SearchBelief)`. New field `predicate: Option<String>` on `ToolCall::SearchBelief`: `None` returns audit-friendly full triples (preserves v4.0.37 contract); `Some(p)` returns the object string only (single-active-fact invariant honoured, 0 or 1 findings) so callers like `belief_direct_answer` can use the value directly as a slot fill. `ActionPlanner::belief_direct_answer` builds a minimal `ToolContext` (only `belief` populated), dispatches `SearchBelief { subject: USER_SELF_KEY, predicate: Some(slot) }`, takes the single finding. | v4.1.2 | **Tools as execution, step 2 (reasoning path)** ‚ÄĒ second v4.1.x patch. Same pattern as v4.1.1, applied to reasoning. Pre-v4.1.2 `inject_reasoning_chain` did its own filter + score + IsA-depth tiebreak + render; audit-mode `Tool::dispatch(RunLocalReasoner)` shadowed it with a simpler "top 3 triples" picker that had no IsA-depth knowledge ‚ÄĒ could disagree on tie-breaks. Now `Tool::RunLocalReasoner` *is* the picker + renderer. `ToolCall::RunLocalReasoner` gains `curated_only: bool` field. Dispatcher does the full pipeline (filter + safety + score + IsA-depth tiebreak + canonical-triple tiebreak + `render_derivation_as_kazakh`) and returns the single rendered chain. `inject_reasoning_chain` becomes a thin wrapper that dispatches the tool, captures the rendered finding, writes to `intent.reasoning_chain`, returns the `ToolResult` for trace audit. `score_derivation`, `render_derivation_as_kazakh`, free `isa_chain_depth(extracted, subject, target)` are now `pub(crate)`; `Conversation::isa_chain_depth` method wrapper removed. Redundant audit-mode `RunLocalReasoner` dispatch removed. **Reply text byte-identical**; cognitive baseline 22/22 unchanged | 577 (unchanged) |
| v4.1.1 | **Tools as execution, step 1 (retrieval path)** ‚ÄĒ first v4.1.x patch. Begins the tools-as-execution migration. Pre-v4.1.1 `inject_retrieval_example` called `MorphemeIndex::rank` directly; the audit-mode `Tool::dispatch(SearchRetrieval)` shadowed it with a duplicate call that used a hardcoded `RankConfig::default()` instead of the conversation's actual `rank_config`. Now `inject_retrieval_example` *is* the tool dispatch: `ToolContext` gains `rank_config: Option<&RankConfig>`; `Tool::SearchRetrieval` honours it; `inject_retrieval_example` calls `Tool::dispatch(SearchRetrieval { morphemes })`, takes first finding, falls back to v1.6.5 single-morpheme postings lookup if empty, returns `ToolResult` for the caller to record on `TurnTrace.tool_calls`. Redundant audit-mode `SearchRetrieval` dispatch removed; `SearchBelief` / `RunLocalReasoner` audit dispatches unchanged for now. **Reply text byte-identical**; cognitive baseline 22/22 unchanged | 577 (unchanged) |

| v4.0.30 | **Turn-counter fix + ReadyToAnswer reachability (Codex v4.0.29 review)** ‚ÄĒ two invariant fixes on Phase 2 substrate before Phase 3 builds on top. **#1 (High, Codex)**: pre-v4.0.30 turn ids came from `intent_history.len()` which caps at `MAX_HISTORY = 32`, so `goal_set_at_turn` / `recorded_at_turn` / `detected_at_turn` plateaued after 32 turns. **Fix**: `Conversation::turn_counter: usize` monotone unbounded counter; threaded into `absorb_entities(intent, turn_id)` and `task.roll_forward(..., turn_id)`; saturating-add; cleared on reset. | v4.0.28 | **BeliefState single-active-fact invariant fix (Codex v4.0.27 review #1)** ‚ÄĒ Codex's v4.0.27 external review found a real invariant bug in the Phase 1 substrate before Phase 2 could start. **Bug**: sequence `value ‚Üí same value ‚Üí different value` left the first copy `Active`, so `active_fact()` returned a stale winner even after a contradiction was logged. Pre-v4.0.28 `record_user_fact` used `rposition` and flipped only the most recent active fact. Blocker for Phase 2+ because TaskState / ActionPlanner / Verifier will trust `active_fact()` as authoritative. **Fix**: rewrote to snapshot every prior `Active` fact for `(subject, predicate)` and flip all in one sweep. New invariant enforced by construction ‚ÄĒ at most one `Active` per `(subject, predicate)` at any time. **Tests**: renamed + tightened `repeated_same_value_preserves_single_active_invariant` (was: both Active, now: fact[0] Superseded + fact[1] Active); new unit `same_same_different_leaves_no_active_fact` (Codex's exact repro) ‚ÄĒ asserts `active_fact() == None` + 0 active + 1 conflict; new integration `same_same_different_city_leaves_no_active_fact_via_conversation` through full `Conversation::turn` pipeline | 505 tests (+2 invariant regression) |
| v4.0.27 | **BeliefState foundation (Codex v4.0.26 roadmap Phase 1)** ‚ÄĒ first architectural patch on Codex's v5.0 roadmap. Starts shift from reactive answering to goal-directed cognition. **Non-breaking**: new `crates/adam-dialog/src/belief.rs` (~540 lines). Types: `BeliefState { entities, facts, pending_questions, contradictions }`, `BeliefFact { subject/predicate/object, confidence, provenance, status, recorded_at_turn }`, `ConfidenceBand { Confirmed/Derived/Retrieved/Hypothesized/Unknown }`, `Provenance { UserStatement/Retrieval/Reasoning/Curated }`, `FactStatus { Active/Superseded/Contested }`, `EntityMemory`, `EntityKind`, `QuestionNature`, `BeliefConflict`, sentinel `USER_SELF_KEY = "__self__"`. Core API: `record_user_fact(subject, predicate, object, turn_id)` ‚ÄĒ appends new fact, detects contradictions (flips both sides to `Contested`, logs `BeliefConflict`, pushes `PendingQuestion::ContradictionToResolve`); `touch_entity` tracks first/last seen + aliases; `active_fact`, `digest`. **Wiring**: `Conversation` gains `belief: BeliefState` field; `absorb_entities` dual-writes to both legacy `session` map and new belief state (turn id = `intent_history.len()`); `reset()` clears belief; `TurnTrace` carries `belief_digest` + `belief_snapshot`; `adam_chat --trace` prints digest line + explicit conflict entries. **Smoke-test**: two contradictory city statements produce `contested=2 pending=1 conflicts=1` in trace; reply text unchanged (substrate only ‚ÄĒ later phases use the state to modify answers). 9 new tests (6 unit + 3 integration). **Out of scope**: roadmap Phases 2‚Äď7 (TaskState, ActionPlanner, Verifier, UncertaintyPolicy, ToolLayer, CognitiveEval) ‚ÄĒ each future release gets its own review cycle; no commitment to the full 7 yet | 503 tests (+9 belief) |

| v4.0.14 | **R10 InDomain-inheritance via IsA ‚ÄĒ new reasoning rule (reasoner roster 8 ‚Üí 9)** ‚ÄĒ second consecutive rule-axis patch. Pattern `A IsA B ‚ąß B InDomain D ‚üĻ A InDomain D` (identical shape to R2 Has-inheritance). | v4.0.8 | **`extract_facts --world-core-only` fast-path ‚ÄĒ throughput infrastructure** ‚ÄĒ one-time patch closing the main inefficiency the user flagged at v4.0.7 ("2 —á–į—Ā–į –Ĺ–į –ĺ–ī–ł–Ĺ –Ņ–į—ā—á —Ā–ł–Ľ—Ć–Ĺ–ĺ —Ä–į—Ā—ā–ĺ—á–ł—ā–Ķ–Ľ—Ć–Ĺ–ĺ"). Previous v4.0.3 ‚Üí v4.0.7 each spent ~45 min on a full 200k-sample text-pack re-extract that produced the same text-facts every time and only differed in the `world_core/` slice. New `--world-core-only` flag on `extract_facts`: (1) read committed `facts.json`, (2) `retain` every fact whose `source.pack` does NOT start with `world_core/`, (3) re-load `data/world_core/*.jsonl` via existing `load_world_core_facts`, (4) merge + recompute `by_predicate` / `by_pack` from scratch, (5) stamp `status: "world_core_refresh"` (new sentinel value, first-class per v3.1.0 iteration contract). Mutually exclusive with `--full` / `--bench-order` / `--max-total` (fails fast). **Measured equivalence**: baseline v4.0.7 `facts.json` (2 476 s elapsed) vs fast-path output ‚ÄĒ byte-identical save for `status` + `elapsed_s` (both intentional markers). Every one of 13 745 facts, every count, every source chain match exactly. **Measured throughput**: full extract ~41 min (2 476 s) ‚Üí fast-path <1 s (2.5 s with cargo startup) = **~1 500√ó speedup** on world_core-only patches. Unblocks the "batch 3‚Äď5 domains per patch" direction the user flagged at v4.0.7: 5 domains rebuild in seconds instead of 4 √ó 45 min = 3 h of serial re-extraction. Guardrail: correct ONLY when text-extraction output is unchanged ‚ÄĒ any patch touching pattern matchers, lexicon, or corpus MUST still run a full extract. Single-concern patch: one flag, one helper, zero extractor changes, zero new predicates, **463 tests (unchanged ‚ÄĒ correctness baseline preserved)** | 463 tests (unchanged); first tooling-throughput patch in v4.x, enables axis-rotation rhythm at sustainable cost |

| v3.8.5 | **Precision hardening ‚ÄĒ Codex review response (scaling ladder step 8.5)** ‚ÄĒ patch release closing three categories of defect the external reviewer flagged on v3.8.0. **(1) Doc drift**: removed contradicting README row (`4/5 active rules` vs `3 (R1/R2/R5)` in the same table); architecture_v3 matcher table rewritten from 4 matchers to 11, R3 marked `active (v3.5.5)`, added R6/R7 as v3.9+ targets. **(2) Renderer morphology**: `render_derivation_as_kazakh` (both in `conversation` and in `adam_inspect`) was dash-concatenating case suffixes ‚ÄĒ `format!("{}-“ď–į", root)` ‚ÄĒ producing invalid Kazakh like `–į—ā–į—É-“ď–į` (broken dash AND front-harmony roots stuck with back -“ď–į). v3.8.5 routes every case suffix through `synthesise_noun(root, features)` so –į—ā–į—É‚Üí–į—ā–į—É“ď–į, ”©—Ā—Ė–ľ–ī—Ė–ļ‚Üí”©—Ā—Ė–ľ–ī—Ė–ļ–ļ–Ķ, “õ–į–∑–į“õ‚Üí“õ–į–∑–į“õ“õ–į (with gemination). Regression test asserts positive FST form + negative dash absence. Known limitation discovered: FST genitive-after-vowel produces `“õ–į–Ľ–į–ī—č“£` instead of `“õ–į–Ľ–į–Ĺ—č“£` (deep phonology defect deferred to v3.9); renderer sidesteps by using dative/ablative in PartOf/Causes chains. **(3) Matcher precision**: added `is_location_root` (50-toponym allow-list) + `is_time_noun` (22 time words) + expanded `is_closed_class` with `–ľ“Ī–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ/—Ā–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ/–ĺ–Ĺ–ī–į–Ļ/–ļ–Ķ–Ļ–Ī—Ė—Ä/”©–∑/”©–∑—Ė/‚Ä¶`. Refuses country subjects for LivesIn (“ö–į–∑–į“õ—Ā—ā–į–Ĺ can't reside), time-noun subjects for LivesIn/GoesTo/DoesTo (–ļ“Į–Ĺ ‚Üí goes_to ‚Üí –∂“Ī–ľ—č—Ā was 16.6 % of all GoesTo), demonstrative subjects across the board. Also rejects LivesIn/GoesTo objects whose FST analysis retains a P3 possessive (fragment parses like `–į—É–ľ–į“ď—č–Ĺ`). Minimum subject-root length 3 chars. **(4) Demo preview/actual mismatch**: `adam_demo` Part 4 preview claimed `–Ĺ–Ķ–ľ—Ė—Ā ‚Üí —Ö–į–Ľ“õ—č` but rendered `–Ĺ–Ķ–ľ—Ė—Ā ‚Üí –į—Ä–į`. Root cause: demo selected by BTreeMap(rule_id) but `inject_reasoning_chain` used `find(subj==probe || obj==probe)`. Fixed both sides ‚ÄĒ `inject_reasoning_chain` now strict subject-first two-pass; demo skips derivations whose subject was claimed by an earlier derivation in storage order. 7 new tests (423 total, from 416) | 423 workspace tests (+7); precision + auditability bumped to make v3.9 investor demos credible |
| v3.8.0 | **Critical verb-root bug fix: LivesIn + GoesTo activated (scaling ladder step 8)** ‚ÄĒ two dormant predicates silently broken since v2.1 / v2.5 respectively. Root-comparison used Kazakh infinitive (`"—ā“Ī—Ä—É"` / `"–Ī–į—Ä—É"`) but FST stores verb stems without `-—É` suffix (`"—ā“Ī—Ä"` / `"–Ī–į—Ä"`). Neither matcher has ever fired, at any scale. Fix: comparison now uses FST stems; widened LivesIn to `{—ā“Ī—Ä, –ľ–Ķ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ, –ĺ—Ä–Ĺ–į–Ľ–į—Ā}`, GoesTo to `{–Ī–į—Ä, –ļ–Ķ–Ľ}`. ## Pre-Phase-10 ‚ÄĒ transformer era (v0.1.0 ‚Üí v0.4.0)

Historical context for readers who want the full lineage. None of the code or data on this path is load-bearing for v1.0.0 except where explicitly referenced (the v0.4.0 checkpoint, the corpus packs consumed by `validate_foundation.sh`).

- **Phase 6 (v0.1.1 ‚Äď v0.1.6)** ‚ÄĒ authentic Kazakh source ingestion: Tatoeba (4,058), Kazakh Wikipedia (15,000), Common Voice KK (6,108). Unified corpus reaches 39 k samples, lossless tokenization at 0 unknowns / 100% roundtrip.
- **Phase 7 (v0.1.3 ‚Äď v0.2.0)** ‚ÄĒ transformer baselines on real text. 4.28 M-parameter envelope saturates by v0.2.0 (PPL ~1100 flat); capacity, not data, is the bottleneck.
- **Phase 8 (v0.3.0)** ‚ÄĒ scale to 20 M params. First non-flat PPL delta since real-text onset (PPL 871). 20 M is the largest config fitting M2 8 GB unified memory.
- **Phase 9 (v0.4.0)** ‚ÄĒ 24.2 M transformer with literary sources (Abai Wikisource 2,253 samples) + CC-100 web-crawl (50 k filtered) + synthetic-generator min-length raised to 3 words + BPE vocab 4k ‚Üí 8k. Val PPL 1691.89 on 12,101 held-out samples. Confirmed capacity limit: 24 M √ó 4 M tokens is ‚Čą 25√ó below Chinchilla-optimal.

The post-v0.4.0 pivot was a deliberate choice: further transformer scaling required an order-of-magnitude more data that didn't exist for Kazakh at the quality bar required. The deterministic FST + dialog path delivered MVP-grade predictable Kazakh in pure Rust on the same hardware.

## Post-v1.0 direction

Post-v1.0.0 testing exposed that the MVP was a programmed toy ‚ÄĒ it answered only the 25 scenarios we enumerated, with no generalisation. The user approved a honest course correction and a long-term commitment to a truly thinking Kazakh model.

### Course-correction rationale

- **v0.9.6 multilingual was a mistake.** The Russian / English triggers diluted the Kazakh-first thesis. A Russian speaker writing "–Į —Ä–į–∑—Ä–į–Ī–ĺ—ā—á–ł–ļ" got "—ā“Į—Ā—Ė–Ĺ–Ī–Ķ–ī—Ė–ľ" because "—Ä–į–∑—Ä–į–Ī–ĺ—ā—á–ł–ļ" wasn't in the Lexicon ‚ÄĒ the recogniser widened the surface without adding real coverage.
- **Fundamental trade-off acknowledged.** Rule-based systems can't generalise; neural systems can but hallucinate. You can't have both. The v1.0.0 predictable pipeline is kept, and generalisation will come as a neural **fallback** for `Intent::Unknown` only ‚ÄĒ the 26-intent deterministic backbone stays as the 0-hallucination guarantee.

### Committed sequence

- **v1.1.0 (done)** ‚ÄĒ Kazakh-only revert; modern Lexicon expansion (+12 roots); Insult intent; smart Unknown handler with noun-hint. Incremental coverage without abandoning thesis.
- **v1.x** ‚ÄĒ Kazakh corpus engineering. **Committed 4.01 M / local 77.9 M as of v1.5.0 (gap to 100 M = 1.3√ó)**. Target: **100 M+ Kazakh tokens** from native-text sources (Qazaq Wikipedia, literature, government Kazakh, OCR books). v1.5.5 government sources are expected to close the gap. Pure data engineering, not ML.
- **v2.0** ‚ÄĒ compact Kazakh LM (transformer or SSM), trained in pure Rust (GGML-style, no PyTorch). Plugged in as the `Intent::Unknown` fallback only. The 26-intent pipeline continues to handle everything it recognises at 0 hallucinations.
- **post-v2.0** ‚ÄĒ multimodality (speech / vision) only after a truly thinking Kazakh LM exists. Not before.

### Post-v1.1.0 candidates (not promised, not scheduled)

- Native-speaker review of the template set (phrasing, register, naturalness).
- Further modern Lexicon expansion (50+ new professions + tech vocabulary).
- Verb slot expansion (`{root|verb_features}` with verb synthesiser dispatch).
- Additional intents beyond the current 26.

## Out of scope (permanent)

- **Multilingual input and output** (v1.1.0 revert). The v0.9.6 Russian / English triggers were removed. `adam` accepts and produces only Kazakh. Generalisation comes via the v2.0 Kazakh LM, not translation.
- **Speech / multimodal** ‚ÄĒ deferred until a thinking Kazakh LM exists.
- **Cloud platform work.**
- **50 M+ parameter transformer experiments on current hardware** (M2 8 GB). Target for v2.0 is a compact model that fits on this hardware.
- **Probabilistic / LLM-style free generation in the recognised-intent path.** The 26-intent deterministic backbone never hallucinates. Only the `Unknown`-fallback path (v2.0) is allowed to be generative, and responses from that path will be explicitly marked in traces.
